<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en"><span dir="auto">Celine Dion albums discography</span></h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">

<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1541" data-file-width="1171" height="329" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg/250px-Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg/375px-Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg/500px-Celine_Dion_Concert_Singing_Taking_Chances_2008.jpg 2x" width="250"/></a><br/>
<span style="line-height:1.1em;">Dion performing "<a href="/wiki/Taking_Chances_(song)" title="Taking Chances (song)">Taking Chances</a>" at her <a href="/wiki/Taking_Chances_World_Tour" title="Taking Chances World Tour">Taking Chances World Tour</a> concert in <a href="/wiki/Bell_Centre" title="Bell Centre">Bell Centre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, Canada on 19 August 2008</span></td>

<p>Canadian singer <a href="/wiki/Celine_Dion" title="Celine Dion">Celine Dion</a> has released twenty-five <a href="/wiki/Album#Studio_album" title="Album">studio albums</a>, seven <a href="/wiki/Live_album" title="Live album">live albums</a>, seventeen <a href="/wiki/Compilation_album" title="Compilation album">compilation albums</a>, and twenty <a href="/wiki/Box_set" title="Box set">box sets</a>. Her debut album, <i><a href="/wiki/La_voix_du_bon_Dieu" title="La voix du bon Dieu">La voix du bon Dieu</a></i> was issued in 1981. In the '80s, Dion released her French-language albums in Canada, with several compilation albums issued also in France. Her first English-language album, entitled <i><a href="/wiki/Unison_(Celine_Dion_album)" title="Unison (Celine Dion album)">Unison</a></i> was released in 1990 and has sold over three million copies worldwide.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-unison_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-unison-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup> It was followed by <i><a href="/wiki/Dion_chante_Plamondon" title="Dion chante Plamondon">Dion chante Plamondon</a></i> in 1991 and <i><a href="/wiki/Celine_Dion_(album)" title="Celine Dion (album)">Celine Dion</a></i> in 1992. The latter became one of six of her albums to be certified <a href="/wiki/Music_Canada#Certification_awards" title="Music Canada">Diamond</a> in Canada for shipments of at least one million units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cria_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-cria-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup> Dion's popularity became well-established with her 1993 album, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Colour_of_My_Love" title="The Colour of My Love">The Colour of My Love</a></i>, which topped the charts in various countries, including the United Kingdom, Canada, and Australia, and has sold twenty million copies around the world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thecolourofmylove_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-thecolourofmylove-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup> In the United States, it was certified <a href="/wiki/RIAA_certification" title="RIAA certification">six-times Platinum</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-riaa_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-riaa-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> Released in 1995, <i><a href="/wiki/D%27eux" title="D'eux">D'eux</a></i> became the best-selling French-language album in history, with sales of ten million copies worldwide.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-deux_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-deux-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup> In France alone, <i>D'eux</i> spent forty-four weeks at the top of the chart and has sold 4.4 million units, becaming the best-selling album of all time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> It also became Dion's first out of five <a href="/wiki/Syndicat_National_de_l%27%C3%89dition_Phonographique#Certification_awards" title="Syndicat National de l'Édition Phonographique">Diamond</a>-certified albums in France.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-snep_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-snep-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Falling_into_You" title="Falling into You">Falling into You</a></i> (1996) and <i><a href="/wiki/Let%27s_Talk_About_Love" title="Let's Talk About Love">Let's Talk About Love</a></i> (1997) were major successes for Dion, both reaching number-one in many countries around the world, and becoming two of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_albums" title="List of best-selling albums">best-selling albums of all time</a>, with sales of over thirty-two and thirty-one million copies, respectively.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fallingintoyou_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-fallingintoyou-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-letstalkaboutlove_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-letstalkaboutlove-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup> Both albums were certified <a href="/wiki/RIAA_certification" title="RIAA certification">Diamond</a> in the United States, with <i>Falling into You</i> achieving later <a href="/wiki/RIAA_certification" title="RIAA certification">eleven-times Platinum</a> certification for shipments of eleven million units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-riaa_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-riaa-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> <i>Falling into You</i> also won the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Album_of_the_Year" title="Grammy Award for Album of the Year">Grammy Award for Album of the Year</a> and <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_Pop_Vocal_Album" title="Grammy Award for Best Pop Vocal Album">Best Pop Vocal Album</a> in 1997.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup> <i>Let's Talk About Love</i> became the first album certified <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_the_Phonographic_Industry#Record_sales_certification" title="International Federation of the Phonographic Industry">ten-times Platinum</a> by the <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_the_Phonographic_Industry" title="International Federation of the Phonographic Industry">IFPI</a> for sales of at least ten million copies in Europe.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-europeancerts_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-europeancerts-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup> In 1998, Dion released another French-language album, <i><a href="/wiki/S%27il_suffisait_d%27aimer" title="S'il suffisait d'aimer">S'il suffisait d'aimer</a></i> and her first English-language <a href="/wiki/Christmas_music" title="Christmas music">holiday album</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/These_Are_Special_Times" title="These Are Special Times">These Are Special Times</a></i>, which became the fourth <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_Christmas/holiday_albums_in_the_United_States" title="List of best-selling Christmas/holiday albums in the United States">best-selling Christmas album in the United States</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Nielsen_SoundScan" title="Nielsen SoundScan">Nielsen SoundScan</a> era, with sales of 5,320,000 copies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-uscurrent_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-uscurrent-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thesearespecialtimes1_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-thesearespecialtimes1-14"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup> Worldwide, it has sold twelve million units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thesearespecialtimes2_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-thesearespecialtimes2-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> A greatest hits compilation with seven new recordings, <i><a href="/wiki/All_the_Way..._A_Decade_of_Song" title="All the Way... A Decade of Song">All the Way... A Decade of Song</a></i> was issued in November 1999, topping the charts around the world, and selling over seventeen million copies, globally, up to January 2002.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-alltheway_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-alltheway-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup> In the United States, <i>All the Way... A Decade of Song</i> became the best-selling greatest hits album by a female artist in the Nielsen SoundScan era where it topped the eight million sales mark.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ussalesfeb2013_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-ussalesfeb2013-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup> In Japan, it was certified <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_Japan#RIAJ_Certification" title="Recording Industry Association of Japan">two-times Million</a> for shipments of two million copies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-riaj_18-0"><a href="#cite_note-riaj-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In March 2002, after a two-year break, Dion returned to music with the album, <i><a href="/wiki/A_New_Day_Has_Come" title="A New Day Has Come">A New Day Has Come</a></i>, which topped the charts in many countries and has sold twelve million copies, worldwide.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-anewdayhascome_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-anewdayhascome-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup> During the five year run of her <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas_Strip" title="Las Vegas Strip">Las Vegas</a> residency show, <i><a href="/wiki/A_New_Day..." title="A New Day...">A New Day...</a></i>, Dion released five studio albums: <i><a href="/wiki/One_Heart" title="One Heart">One Heart</a></i> (2003), <i><a href="/wiki/1_fille_%26_4_types" title="1 fille &amp; 4 types">1 fille &amp; 4 types</a></i> (2003), <i><a href="/wiki/Miracle_(Celine_Dion_album)" title="Miracle (Celine Dion album)">Miracle</a></i> (2004), <i><a href="/wiki/D%27elles" title="D'elles">D'elles</a></i> (2007) and <i><a href="/wiki/Taking_Chances" title="Taking Chances">Taking Chances</a></i> (2007). After <a href="/wiki/Taking_Chances_World_Tour" title="Taking Chances World Tour">Taking Chances World Tour</a> and another break, she started her second Las Vegas residency show, <i><a href="/wiki/Celine_(residency_show)" title="Celine (residency show)">Celine</a></i> in March 2011. In 2012, Dion began recording songs for her new French and English-language albums. <i><a href="/wiki/Sans_attendre" title="Sans attendre">Sans attendre</a></i> was released in November 2012 and topped the charts in Francophone countries. It became the best-selling album of 2012 in France where it was certified Diamond.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-snep_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-snep-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Loved_Me_Back_to_Life" title="Loved Me Back to Life">Loved Me Back to Life</a></i> was issued in November 2013 and became Dion's thirteenth number-one album in the Nielsen SoundScan era in Canada and eleventh to debut at the top of the chart.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup> It also reached number two in the United States, and number three in the United Kingdom and France. <i>Loved Me Back to Life</i> was certified <a href="/wiki/Music_Canada#Certification_awards" title="Music Canada">four-times Platinum</a> in Canada, <a href="/wiki/Syndicat_National_de_l%27%C3%89dition_Phonographique#Certification_awards" title="Syndicat National de l'Édition Phonographique">two-times Platinum</a> in France and <a href="/wiki/British_Phonographic_Industry#BPI_Certified_Awards_programme" title="British Phonographic Industry">Platinum</a> in the United Kingdom.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cria_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-cria-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-snep_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-snep-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bpi_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-bpi-22"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup> In August 2014, Dion announced the indefinite postponement of all her show business activities, due to the worsening of her husband's health after he underwent the removal of a cancerous tumor in December 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Dion has sold more than 220 million albums worldwide and is recognized as one of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_music_artists" title="List of best-selling music artists">world's best-selling music artists</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2004, she received the <a href="/wiki/Chopard_Diamond_award" title="Chopard Diamond award">Chopard Diamond Award</a> at the <a href="/wiki/World_Music_Awards" title="World Music Awards">World Music Awards</a> recognizing her status as the best-selling female artist of all time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-worldawards_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-worldawards-25"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2007, Dion was honored with the <a href="/wiki/World_Music_Awards#Legend_Awards" title="World Music Awards">Legend Award</a> at the World Music Awards in recognition of her global success and outstanding contribution to the music industry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-worldawards_25-1"><a href="#cite_note-worldawards-25"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup> She is the best-selling Canadian artist in history, the best-selling artist in the Nielsen SoundScan era in Canada (from 1995) and the second best-selling female artist of the Nielsen SoundScan era in the United States (from 1991), with album sales of 52,234,000 copies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup> Her albums <i>Falling into You</i>, <i>Let's Talk About Love</i>, <i>All the Way... A Decade of Song</i>, <i>The Colour of My Love</i> and <i>These Are Special Times</i> are among the top 100 certified albums according to the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">RIAA</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Studio_albums">Studio albums</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Celine_Dion_albums_discography&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Studio albums">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1980s">1980s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Celine_Dion_albums_discography&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1980s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table border="1" class="wikitable plainrowheaders" style="text-align:center;">
<tr>
<th rowspan="2" style="width:15em;">Title</th>
<th rowspan="2" style="width:17em;">Album details</th>
<th colspan="10">Peak chart positions</th>
<th rowspan="2" style="width:12em;">Sales</th>
<th rowspan="2" style="width:12em;"><a href="/wiki/List_of_music_recording_certifications" title="List of music recording certifications">Certifications</a></th>
</tr>
<tr style="font-size:smaller;">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Celine_Dion_albums_discography&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><sup><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_a"><b><a href="#ref_a">^[a]</a></b></span></sup> position on the Music DVD Chart</li>
<li><sup><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_b"><b><a href="#ref_b">^[b]</a></b></span></sup> French-language version certified Diamond and English-language version certified 4× Platinum</li>
<li><sup><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_c"><b><a href="#ref_c">^[c]</a></b></span></sup> certified as video</li>
</ul>
